    PROCEDURE UpdateSurcharge@1100529500(CostType@1100485000 : Integer);
    VAR
      RcpLineRec@1100525000 : Record 11072075;
      EstSetup@1100529400 : Record 11012150;
    BEGIN
      //C033781
      EstSetup.GET;
      IF EstSetup."Apply Surcharge Recipe Header" = EstSetup."Apply Surcharge Recipe Header"::Cumulative THEN EXIT;

      RcpLineRec.SETRANGE("Estimate No.","Estimate No.");
      RcpLineRec.SETRANGE("Sub-Estimate No.","Sub-Estimate No.");
      RcpLineRec.SETRANGE("Part Group","Part Group");
      RcpLineRec.SETRANGE(Part,Part);
      RcpLineRec.SETRANGE("Estimate Line","Line No.");
      RcpLineRec.SETRANGE("Surcharge Type", RcpLineRec."Surcharge Type"::" ");
      RcpLineRec.SETRANGE("Recipe Header", FALSE);
      IF CostType = 0 THEN
        RcpLineRec.SETFILTER("Surcharge % Labor", '%1|%2', 0, xRec."Surcharge % Labor");
      IF CostType = 1 THEN
        RcpLineRec.SETFILTER("Surcharge % Price", '%1|%2', 0, xRec."Recipe Surcharge % Material");
      IF CostType = 2 THEN
        RcpLineRec.SETFILTER("Surcharge % Price", '%1|%2', 0, xRec."Recipe Surcharge % Subc.");
      IF CostType = 3 THEN
        RcpLineRec.SETFILTER("Surcharge % Price", '%1|%2', 0, xRec."Recipe Surcharge % Plant");
      IF CostType = 4 THEN
        RcpLineRec.SETFILTER("Surcharge % Price", '%1|%2', 0, xRec."Recipe Surcharge % Sundry");
      IF RcpLineRec.FINDSET(TRUE, FALSE) THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          IF CostType = 0 THEN
            RcpLineRec.VALIDATE("Surcharge % Labor", "Surcharge % Labor");
          IF CostType = 1 THEN
            IF RcpLineRec."Cost Type (Price)" = RcpLineRec."Cost Type (Price)"::Material THEN
              RcpLineRec.VALIDATE("Surcharge % Price", "Recipe Surcharge % Material");
          IF CostType = 2 THEN
            IF RcpLineRec."Cost Type (Price)" = RcpLineRec."Cost Type (Price)"::Subcontracting THEN
              RcpLineRec.VALIDATE("Surcharge % Price", "Recipe Surcharge % Subc.");
          IF CostType = 3 THEN
            IF RcpLineRec."Cost Type (Price)" = RcpLineRec."Cost Type (Price)"::Plant THEN
              RcpLineRec.VALIDATE("Surcharge % Price", "Recipe Surcharge % Plant");
          IF CostType = 4 THEN
            IF RcpLineRec."Cost Type (Price)" = RcpLineRec."Cost Type (Price)"::Sundry THEN
              RcpLineRec.VALIDATE("Surcharge % Price", "Recipe Surcharge % Sundry");
          RcpLineRec.MODIFY;
        UNTIL RcpLineRec.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      //(update recipe-child header)
      RcpLineRec.SETRANGE("Estimate No.","Estimate No.");
      RcpLineRec.SETRANGE("Sub-Estimate No.","Sub-Estimate No.");
      RcpLineRec.SETRANGE("Part Group","Part Group");
      RcpLineRec.SETRANGE(Part,Part);
      RcpLineRec.SETRANGE("Estimate Line","Line No.");
      RcpLineRec.SETRANGE("Surcharge Type", RcpLineRec."Surcharge Type"::" ");
      RcpLineRec.SETRANGE("Recipe Header", TRUE);
      IF CostType = 0 THEN
        RcpLineRec.SETFILTER("Surcharge % Labor", '%1|%2', 0, xRec."Surcharge % Labor");
      IF CostType = 1 THEN
        RcpLineRec.SETFILTER("Recipe Surcharge % Material", '%1|%2', 0, xRec."Recipe Surcharge % Material");
      IF CostType = 2 THEN
        RcpLineRec.SETFILTER("Recipe Surcharge % Subc.", '%1|%2', 0, xRec."Recipe Surcharge % Subc.");
      IF CostType = 3 THEN
        RcpLineRec.SETFILTER("Recipe Surcharge % Plant", '%1|%2', 0, xRec."Recipe Surcharge % Plant");
      IF CostType = 4 THEN
        RcpLineRec.SETFILTER("Recipe Surcharge % Sundry", '%1|%2', 0, xRec."Recipe Surcharge % Sundry");
      IF RcpLineRec.FINDSET(TRUE, FALSE) THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          IF CostType = 0 THEN
            RcpLineRec.VALIDATE("Surcharge % Labor", "Surcharge % Labor");
          IF CostType = 1 THEN
            RcpLineRec.VALIDATE("Recipe Surcharge % Material", "Recipe Surcharge % Material");
          IF CostType = 2 THEN
            RcpLineRec.VALIDATE("Recipe Surcharge % Subc.", "Recipe Surcharge % Subc.");
          IF CostType = 3 THEN
            RcpLineRec.VALIDATE("Recipe Surcharge % Plant", "Recipe Surcharge % Plant");
          IF CostType = 4 THEN
            RcpLineRec.VALIDATE("Recipe Surcharge % Sundry", "Recipe Surcharge % Sundry");
          RcpLineRec.MODIFY;
        UNTIL RcpLineRec.NEXT = 0;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE RecalculateSurcharge@1100529501();
    VAR
      RcpLineRec@1100529401 : Record 11072075;
    BEGIN
      //C033781
      RcpLineRec.SETRANGE("Estimate No.","Estimate No.");
      RcpLineRec.SETRANGE("Sub-Estimate No.","Sub-Estimate No.");
      RcpLineRec.SETRANGE("Part Group","Part Group");
      RcpLineRec.SETRANGE(Part,Part);
      RcpLineRec.SETRANGE("Estimate Line","Line No.");
      IF RcpLineRec.FINDSET(TRUE, FALSE) THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          RcpLineRec.CalculateTotals;
          RcpLineRec.MODIFY;
        UNTIL RcpLineRec.NEXT = 0;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE SetTempEstimate@1100529900(lvEstRec@1100529900 : Record 11012151);
    BEGIN
      //C038554
      EstRec := lvEstRec;
      SkipReadEstimate := TRUE;
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetSubcontractorActivity@1100529901(CalledBy@1100528500 : Integer);
    VAR
      SubcontractingActivityPrice@1100529900 : Record 11229373;
      Estimate@1100525000 : Record 11012151;
    BEGIN
      //DP01492-2
      Estimate.GET("Estimate No.");
      Estimate.TESTFIELD(Fixed, FALSE);  //C041836

      TESTFIELD("Cost Type (Price)", "Cost Type (Price)"::Subcontracting);
      SubcontractingActivityPrice.SETRANGE("Subcontracting Activity", "Subcontracting Activity");
      IF CalledBy = FIELDNO("Subcontracting Activity") THEN  //DP01958a
        SubcontractingActivityPrice.SETRANGE("Preferred Subcontractor", TRUE)
      ELSE
        SubcontractingActivityPrice.SETRANGE("Subcontractor No.", Subcontractor);
      IF SubcontractingActivityPrice.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
        VALIDATE("Net Cost Price", SubcontractingActivityPrice.GetPrice(Estimate."Reference Date (Rate)"));
        IF CalledBy = FIELDNO("Subcontracting Activity") THEN BEGIN  //DP01958a
          SubcontractingActivityPrice.CALCFIELDS("Activity Description");
          Description := SubcontractingActivityPrice."Activity Description";
        END;
        "Unit of Measure" := SubcontractingActivityPrice."Unit of Measure";
        "Cost Object Price" := SubcontractingActivityPrice."Cost Object";
        Subcontractor := SubcontractingActivityPrice."Subcontractor No.";
      END;
      IF "Subcontracting in Hours" THEN BEGIN  //C053751
        "Cost Type (Hours)" := "Cost Type (Hours)"::Subcontracting;
        "Rate Code" := '';
        InitRateRelatedFields;
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE ScalingFactorIsEmpty@1100527210();
    BEGIN
      TESTFIELD("Scaling Factor", 0);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE EntityDefined@1100528500() : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      //C044586
      IF ("Item No." + "Basic Item" + "Trade Item" = '') AND
         ("Sub Operation Code" + "Subcontracting Activity" = '') AND
         ("Plant Type" + "Set Code" = '') THEN
        EXIT(FALSE)
      ELSE
        EXIT(TRUE);
    END;

    PROCEDURE FindLowestPriceTradeItems@1100528404();
    VAR
      TempAlternativeTradeItem@1100528400 : TEMPORARY Record 11012744;
      SourceRecRef@1100528402 : RecordRef;
      LineNo@1100528401 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      IF FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          LineNo := LineNo + 10000;
          TempAlternativeTradeItem.CreateAlternativeTradeItem(
            LineNo, "Trade Item", "Unit of Measure", "Vendor (Trade Item)",
            Quantity, "Currency Code", "Net Cost Price", "Net Cost Price (FCY)",
            "Material Cost Amount", "Material Cost Amount (FCY)", RECORDID, FALSE);
        UNTIL NEXT = 0;

      IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Alternative Trade Items", TempAlternativeTradeItem) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
        IF TempAlternativeTradeItem.FINDSET THEN
          REPEAT
            SourceRecRef.GET(TempAlternativeTradeItem."Source Record ID");
            SourceRecRef.SETTABLE(Rec);
            IF ("Trade Item" <> TempAlternativeTradeItem."Item Code") OR
               ("Vendor (Trade Item)" <> TempAlternativeTradeItem.Vendor)
            THEN BEGIN
              VALIDATE("Trade Item", '');
              IF "Vendor (Trade Item)" <> TempAlternativeTradeItem.Vendor THEN
                VALIDATE("Original Vendor (Trade Item)", "Vendor (Trade Item)");
              VALIDATE("Vendor (Trade Item)", TempAlternativeTradeItem.Vendor);
              VALIDATE("Trade Item", TempAlternativeTradeItem."Item Code");
              MODIFY(TRUE);
            END;
          UNTIL TempAlternativeTradeItem.NEXT = 0;
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE UpdateLinkedRecipe@1100528916();
    VAR
      EstimateLine@1100528900 : Record 11072072;
      EstimateRecipeLine@1100528901 : Record 11072075;
      RecipeProcessed@1100528902 : Boolean;
      SourceLine@1100528903 : Record 11072075;
      TargetLine@1100528904 : Record 11072075;
    BEGIN
      //DP02082
      IF NOT "Linked Recipe" THEN EXIT;

      EstimateLine.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", "Estimate No.");
      EstimateLine.SETRANGE("Recipe Group", "Recipe Group");
      EstimateLine.SETRANGE(Recipe, Recipe);
      EstimateLine.SETRANGE("Linked Recipe", "Linked Recipe");
      EstimateLine.SETRANGE("Recipe Lines Exist", TRUE);
      IF EstimateLine.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          //find first linked recipe with same code which is not current recipe
          IF (EstimateLine."Sub-Estimate No." <> "Sub-Estimate No.") OR
            (EstimateLine."Part Group" <> "Part Group") OR
            (EstimateLine.Part <> Part) OR
            (EstimateLine."Line No." <> "Line No.") THEN
          BEGIN
            EstimateRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", "Estimate No.");
            EstimateRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Sub-Estimate No.", "Sub-Estimate No.");
            EstimateRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Part Group", "Part Group");
            EstimateRecipeLine.SETRANGE(Part, Part);
            EstimateRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Estimate Line", "Line No.");
            IF EstimateRecipeLine.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
              EstimateRecipeLine.SetFromEstimateLineDelete(TRUE);
              REPEAT
                EstimateRecipeLine.DELETE(TRUE);
              UNTIL EstimateRecipeLine.NEXT = 0;
              EstimateRecipeLine.SetFromEstimateLineDelete(FALSE);
            END;
            //
            TargetLine."Estimate No." := "Estimate No.";
            TargetLine."Sub-Estimate No." := "Sub-Estimate No.";
            TargetLine."Part Group" := "Part Group";
            TargetLine.Part := Part;
            TargetLine."Estimate Line" := "Line No.";
            TargetLine."Recipe Group" := "Recipe Group";
            TargetLine.Recipe := Recipe;
            //
            EstimateRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", EstimateLine."Estimate No.");
            EstimateRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Sub-Estimate No.", EstimateLine."Sub-Estimate No.");
            EstimateRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Part Group", EstimateLine."Part Group");
            EstimateRecipeLine.SETRANGE(Part, EstimateLine.Part);
            EstimateRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Estimate Line", EstimateLine."Line No.");
            IF EstimateRecipeLine.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
              REPEAT
                SourceLine := EstimateRecipeLine;
                TargetLine."Line No." := EstimateRecipeLine."Line No.";
                EstimateRecipeLine.CheckLinkedRecipe(4, SourceLine, TargetLine);
              UNTIL EstimateRecipeLine.NEXT = 0;
            END;
            RecipeProcessed := TRUE;
          END;
        UNTIL (EstimateLine.NEXT = 0) OR RecipeProcessed;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE OnAssistEditRecipe@1100528917();
    VAR
      EstimateLine@1100528900 : Record 11072072;
      BaseRecipe@1100528901 : Record 11020581;
      TmpBaseRecipe@1100528902 : TEMPORARY Record 11020581;
    BEGIN
      //DP02082
      EstimateLine.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", "Estimate No.");
      EstimateLine.SETFILTER(Recipe, '<>%1', '');
      IF EstimateLine.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          IF NOT BaseRecipe.GET(EstimateLine."Recipe Group", EstimateLine.Recipe) THEN BEGIN
            IF NOT TmpBaseRecipe.GET(EstimateLine."Recipe Group", EstimateLine.Recipe) THEN BEGIN
              TmpBaseRecipe."Recipe Group" := EstimateLine."Recipe Group";
              TmpBaseRecipe."No." := EstimateLine.Recipe;
              TmpBaseRecipe.INSERT;
              EstimateLine.MARK := TRUE;
            END;
          END;
        UNTIL EstimateLine.NEXT = 0;
        EstimateLine.MARKEDONLY(TRUE);
      END;
      IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Estimate Line List", EstimateLine) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
        "Recipe Group" := EstimateLine."Recipe Group";
        VALIDATE(Recipe, EstimateLine.Recipe);
        Description := EstimateLine.Description;
        "Unit of Measure" := EstimateLine."Unit of Measure";
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE UpdateSalesPricebyRecipe@1100528918();
    VAR
      SalesPricebyEstimate@1100528900 : Record 11229774;
      RefDate@1100528901 : Date;
    BEGIN
      //DP02089
      IF Recipe = '' THEN
        "Sales Price (Recipe)" := 0;
      //
      EstRec.GET("Estimate No.");
      RefDate := EstRec."Reference Date (Sales Price)";
      //
      SalesPricebyEstimate.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", "Estimate No.");
      SalesPricebyEstimate.SETRANGE("Estimate Type", SalesPricebyEstimate."Estimate Type"::Recipe);
      SalesPricebyEstimate.SETRANGE("Recipe Group", "Recipe Group");
      SalesPricebyEstimate.SETRANGE(Recipe, Recipe);
      SalesPricebyEstimate.SETRANGE("Starting Date", 0D, RefDate);
      SalesPricebyEstimate.SETFILTER("Ending Date", '%1|>=%2', 0D, RefDate);
      IF SalesPricebyEstimate.FINDLAST THEN
        "Sales Price (Recipe)" := SalesPricebyEstimate.Price;
    END;

    PROCEDURE AddLineToHeader@1100528504();
    VAR
      EstimateLine@1100528900 : Record 11072072;
      HeaderLine@1100528903 : Record 11072072;
      NextLine@1100528901 : Integer;
      BaseLine@1100528902 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      IF "Line No." = 0 THEN BEGIN
        EstimateLine.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", "Estimate No.");
        EstimateLine.SETRANGE("Sub-Estimate No.", "Sub-Estimate No.");
        EstimateLine.SETRANGE("Part Group", "Part Group");
        EstimateLine.SETRANGE(Part, Part);
        IF NOT EstimateLine.FINDLAST THEN EXIT;
        //
        NextLine := EstimateLine."Line No." + 10000;
        IF (EstimateLine."Plant Type" <> '') OR
           (EstimateLine."Set Code" <> '') THEN
          BaseLine := EstimateLine."Line No.";
        IF EstimateLine."Attached to Line No." <> 0 THEN
          IF EstimateLine.GET("Estimate No.", "Sub-Estimate No.", "Part Group", Part, EstimateLine."Attached to Line No.") THEN
            BaseLine := EstimateLine."Line No.";
      END ELSE BEGIN
        IF ("Plant Type" <> '') OR
           ("Set Code" <> '') THEN
          BaseLine := "Line No.";
        IF "Attached to Line No." <> 0 THEN
          IF EstimateLine.GET("Estimate No.", "Sub-Estimate No.", "Part Group", Part, "Attached to Line No.") THEN
            BaseLine := EstimateLine."Line No.";
        //
        EstimateLine.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", "Estimate No.");
        EstimateLine.SETRANGE("Sub-Estimate No.", "Sub-Estimate No.");
        EstimateLine.SETRANGE("Part Group", "Part Group");
        EstimateLine.SETRANGE(Part, Part);
        EstimateLine.SETFILTER("Line No.", '>%1', "Line No.");
        IF EstimateLine.FINDFIRST THEN
          NextLine := "Line No." + ROUND(((EstimateLine."Line No." - "Line No.")/2),1)
        ELSE
          NextLine := "Line No." + 10000;
      END;

      IF BaseLine = 0 THEN EXIT;
      HeaderLine.GET("Estimate No.", "Sub-Estimate No.", "Part Group", Part, BaseLine);
      //
      EstimateLine.INIT;
      EstimateLine."Estimate No." := "Estimate No.";
      EstimateLine.VALIDATE("Sub-Estimate No.", "Sub-Estimate No.");
      EstimateLine."Part Group" := "Part Group";
      EstimateLine.VALIDATE(Part, Part);
      EstimateLine."Line No." := NextLine;
      EstimateLine.INSERT(TRUE);
      //
      IF (HeaderLine."Plant Type" <> '') OR
         (HeaderLine."Set Code" <> '') THEN BEGIN
        EstimateLine.Description := '<' + FIELDCAPTION("Attached to Line No.") + ': ' + FORMAT(BaseLine) + '>';
        EstimateLine."Attached to Line No." := BaseLine;
        EstimateLine."Set Level" := HeaderLine."Set Level" + 1;
      END;
      EstimateLine.MODIFY;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckBomLines@1100528919();
    VAR
      EstimateLine@1210190000 : Record 11072072;
      OldQuan@1210190001 : Decimal;
      NewQuan@1210190002 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      IF ("BOM Item No." = '') THEN EXIT;
      IF ("Level BOM" <> 0) THEN EXIT;

      //DP02339.sn
      OldQuan := xRec.Quantity;
      NewQuan := Quantity;
      //DP02339.en

      EstimateLine.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", "Estimate No.");
      EstimateLine.SETRANGE("Sub-Estimate No.", "Sub-Estimate No.");
      EstimateLine.SETRANGE("Part Group", "Part Group");
      EstimateLine.SETRANGE(Part, Part);
      EstimateLine.SETRANGE("BOM Item No.", "BOM Item No.");
      EstimateLine.SETRANGE("Part of Line", "Line No.");
      IF EstimateLine.FINDSET(TRUE, FALSE) THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          IF OldQuan = 0 THEN
            EstimateLine.Quantity := EstimateLine."Original Quantity" * NewQuan  //DP02339
          ELSE
            EstimateLine.Quantity := EstimateLine.Quantity * NewQuan / OldQuan;
          EstimateLine.CalculateTotals;
          EstimateLine.MODIFY(TRUE);
        UNTIL EstimateLine.NEXT = 0;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE ActivateCheckFullCostPrice@1100528920();
    VAR
      UserSetup@1100528900 : Record 91;
    BEGIN
      //C057346
      UserSetup.GET(USERID);
      IF UserSetup."Activate Full Cost Price" = FALSE THEN BEGIN
        UserSetup."Activate Full Cost Price" := TRUE;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        UserSetup."Activate Full Cost Price" := FALSE;
      END;
      UserSetup.MODIFY;
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetDisciplineByElement@1100529020();
    VAR
      BaseElement@1100528900 : Record 11012060;
      ProjectElement@1100528901 : Record 11012010;
    BEGIN
      //DP02460
      IF Element = '' THEN EXIT;
      IF "Project No." <> '' THEN BEGIN
        IF NOT ProjectElement.GET("Project No.", Element) THEN ProjectElement.INIT;
        IF ProjectElement.Discipline <> '' THEN
          Discipline := ProjectElement.Discipline;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        IF NOT BaseElement.GET(Element) THEN BaseElement.INIT;
        IF BaseElement.Discipline <> '' THEN
          Discipline := BaseElement.Discipline;
      END;
    END;

    BEGIN
    {
      4PSSE, LAHE 130507 "Price History Found", "Price History Vendor No."
      191010 - Rate code description if no description
      200504 ORANGO.PR Certego Pricefuntion Added Code in Quantity - OnValidate()
    }
    END.
  }
